event = {
id = 901000
random = no
country = AUS
style = 2

trigger = {
exists = HUN
NOT = {
government = communist
ispuppet = AUS

war = { country = AUS country = HUN }
war = { country = AUS country = CZE }
war = { country = AUS country = CRO }
war = { country = HUN country = CRO }
}
}
}

name = "Renegotiating the Ausgleich"
desc = "The Ausgleich was a constitutional compromise between Austria and Hungary negotiated in 1867 after disastrous results of war with Prussia threatened to rip monarchy apart. Every 10 years, the terms of the compromise were renegotiated, usually resulting in internal crisis as the Hungarians gradually escalated their demands towards remaining institution of the central government. It is now time for the 1937 renegotiation of the Ausgleich."
picture = "Peace_conference"

date = { day = 14 month = february year = 1937 }
offset = 10
deathdate = { day = 29 month = february year = 1937 }

action_a = {
ai_chance = 40
name = "Stay with Dualism"
command = { type = relation which = GER value = 50 }
command = { type = relation which = CZE value = -30 }
command = { type = relation which = CRO value = -30 }
command = { type = relation which = GLD value = -30 }
command = { type = relation which = BOS value = -30 }

}

desc = "The Austro-Hungarian government has announced recently that they want to form new alliance block in Europe based upon mutual cooperation and protection between Austria-Hungary and Poland. How shall we respond?"

name = "YES!"

command = { type = trigger which = 901117 }
}

name = "Agree, but demand Galicia"

OR = {
AND = {
control = { province = 235 data = U24 }
control = { province = 242 data = U24 }
NOT = {
exists = GLD
}
}
AND = {
exists = GLD
control = { province = 235 data = GLD }
control = { province = 242 data = GLD }
NOT = { puppet = { country = GLD country = POL } }
}
}
}

command = { type = addcore  which =  238 }

command = { type = addcore  which =  240 }

command = { type = trigger which = 901118 }
}

#  A-H Civil War - Russian Intervention
#########################################################################
event = {
id = 901177
random = no
country = RUS

decision = {
war = { country = AUS country = HUN }
NOT = {
war = { country = RUS country = AUS }
war = { country = RUS country = HUN }
flag = RUS_ISO
exists = SOV
}
OR = {
AND = {
NOT = { exists = UKR }
control = { province = 617 data = RUS }
}
AND = {
exists = UKR
control = { province = 694 data = UKR }
OR = {
alliance = { country = RUS country = UKR }
puppet = { country = UKR country = RUS  }
}
}
}
}

decision_trigger = {
manpower = 10
supplies = 1000
money = 200
}

trigger = {
war = { country = AUS country = HUN }
NOT = {
war = { country = RUS country = AUS }
war = { country = RUS country = HUN }
flag = RUS_ISO
exists = SOV
}
OR = {
AND = {
NOT = { exists = UKR }
control = { province = 617 data = RUS }
}
AND = {
exists = UKR
control = { province = 694 data = UKR }
OR = {
alliance = { country = RUS country = UKR }
puppet = { country = UKR country = RUS  }
}
}
}
}

name = "Civil War in Austria-Hungary!"
desc = "Civil War has erupted in Austria-Hungary following break up of Ausgleich negotiations. This presents us with perfect opportunity to completely rip apart dual monarchy by supporting Hungary with material and volunteers. But some circles in our government argue, that united Austria might be powerful and useful ally in potential contest with German Empire. Who shall we support?"

style = 2
picture = "soviet_reinforcements"
decision_picture = "decision_SCW_German"

date = { day = 1 month = january year = 1936 }
offset = 10
deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1960 }

action_a = {
name = "Support Austria" # Send material and volunteers
ai_chance = 20
command = { type = relation which = AUS value = 20 }
command = { type = relation which = HUN value = -20 }
command = { type = relation which = FRA value = -5 }
command = { type = relation which = ENG value = -5 }
command = { type = relation which = ITA value = -5 }
command = { type = manpowerpool value = -10 }
command = { type = resource which = supplies value = -1000 } # % of max daily income
command = { type = money value = -200 }
command = { type = trigger which = 901178    }
command = { type = belligerence which = RUS value = 1 }
}
action_b = {
name = "Support Hungary" # Send material and volunteers
ai_chance = 40
command = { type = relation which = AUS value = -20 }
command = { type = relation which = HUN value = 20 }
command = { type = relation which = FRA value = -5 }
command = { type = relation which = ENG value = -5 }
command = { type = relation which = ITA value = -5 }
command = { type = manpowerpool value = -10 }
command = { type = resource which = supplies value = -1000 } # % of max daily income
command = { type = money value = -200 }
command = { type = trigger which = 901179   }
command = { type = belligerence which = RUS value = 1 }
}
action_c = {
name = "We must not interfere"
ai_chance = 40
command = { type = relation which = AUS value = -20 }
command = { type = relation which = HUN value = 20 }
command = { type = dissent value = 1 }
command = { type = belligerence which = RUS value = -1 }
}
}

##################################################  #######################
#  Austria-Hungary Civil War ends - An important experience (Russia)
##################################################  #######################
event = {
id = 901180
random = no
country = RUS

trigger = {
OR = {
event = 901178
event = 901179
}
NOT = { war = { country = AUS country = HUN } }
}
name = "The End of the Austro-Hungarian civil war"
desc = "For good or ill, the Austro-Hungarian civil war is now over.  The General Staff have reported that they learnt many valuable lessons regarding the nature of modern warfare over the course of the conflict."


style = 2
picture = "soviet_replacement"

date = { day = 18 month = july year = 1936 }
offset = 50
deathdate = { day = 29 month = december year = 1960 }

action_a = {
name = "ACTIONNAME2803A" # Great!
command = { type = manpowerpool value = 5 }         # Soldiers return home
command = { type = dissent value = -1 }
command = { type = gain_tech which = -1 }         # get random tech blueprints
command = { type = add_leader_skill which = -1 value = 1 }
command = { type = add_leader_skill which = -1 value = 1 }
}
}

Every 10 years, the terms of the compromise were renegotiated, usually resulting in internal crisis as the Hungarians gradually escalated their demands towards remaining institution of the central government. It is now time for the 1947 renegotiation of the Ausgleich."
